# <a name="release-notes-for-beta-channel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-103">Beta 版通道的版本資訊</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-103">Release Notes for Beta Channel</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="c0b70-104">本文包含 Word、Excel、PowerPoint、Outlook、Access 和適用於 Windows 電腦的 Project 的 Beta 版通道組建版本資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-104">This article contains release notes for Beta Channel builds of Word, Excel, PowerPoint, Outlook, Access, and Project for Windows desktop.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-105">每週，我們都會強調有趣的新功能、重要修正，以及我們想讓您知道的重大問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-105">Every week, we'll highlight interesting new features, important fixes, and any significant issues we want you to know about.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-106">請注意，我們通常每隔一段時間會推出 Beta 版通道新功能 (某些時候還有修正)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-106">Note that we often roll out features (and sometimes even fixes) to Beta Channel over a period of time.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-107">這樣可讓我們確保功能都運作順利，然後才推出給更廣泛的對象。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-107">This allows us to ensure that things are working smoothly before releasing the feature to a wider audience.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-108">因此，如果您沒有在以下描述的內容中看到某些項目，請不用擔心，您最終還是會看到它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-108">So, if you don't see something described below, don't worry you'll get it eventually.</span></span>  

> [!IMPORTANT]
> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-109">我們會變更 Microsoft 365 應用程式的更新通道，包括新增新的更新通道 (每月企業通道)，並變更現有的更新通道名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-109">We’re making some changes to the update channels for Microsoft 365 Apps, including adding a new update channel (Monthly Enterprise Channel) and changing the names of the existing update channels.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-110">如需深入了解，[請閱讀本文](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-110">To learn more, [read this article](https://go.microsoft.com/fwlink/p/?linkid=2127441).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-111">版本資訊會每週發佈，可能是多個組建的編譯。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-111">Release notes are posted weekly and may be a compilation of multiple builds.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-112">版本資訊發佈日期可能與實際組建發行日期不相符。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-112">The release notes publication date may not match the actual build release date.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-496">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-496">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-497">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-497">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-498">我們已修正載入儲存的查詢/關聯視窗在捲動時，捲軸位置未正確設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-498">We fixed an issue where scrollbar position was not set correctly when loading query/relationship window saved while scrolled.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-499">我們已修正 [新增表格] 工作窗格未正確顯示包含 '&' 名稱的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-499">We fixed an issue where Add Table Task Pane was not displaying names containing '&' correctly.</span></span>


### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-500">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-500">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-501">我們已修正多層次類別的手動間隔在圖表中無法運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-501">We fixed an issue where multi-level category manual interval was not working in charts.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-502">我們已修正重新整理 OLAP 樞紐分析表時，可能會導致當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-502">We fixed an issue which could cause a hang when refreshing OLAP PivotTables.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-503">我們已修正新增至用於資料驗證之表格，並未更新活頁簿中所有工作表選項的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-503">We fixed an issue where adding to a table used for Data Validation did not update options for all sheets in the workbook.</span></span>


### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-504">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-504">OneNote</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-505">我們已修正 OneNote 在自訂主題的畫布中不會採用高對比色彩的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-505">We fixed an issue where OneNote didn't honor High Contrast colors in the canvas for custom themes.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-506">我們已修正當您將游標移至筆記本色彩選擇器的綠色色彩上方時，快顯會顯示「紅粉色」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-506">We fixed an issue when you hover over green color in notebook color selector, the pop up reads "red chalk".</span></span>


### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-507">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-507">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-508">我們已修正當使用者將來源路徑變更為本機 OneDrive 資料夾時，連結的 Excel 圖表不正確變更為 Excel 工作表的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-508">We fixed an issue where linked excel chart incorrectly changes to excel sheet when user changes the source path to local OneDrive folder.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-523">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-523">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-524">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-524">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-525">修正在使用 2D 地圖圖表時，無法使用 VBA 設定系列中最大值、中間值和最小值顏色的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-525">Fixed an issue with 2D Map Charts where using VBA to set the colors for the max, mid, and min values for a series was not working.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-526">修正當 Office 語言設定為西班牙文時，其中資料驗證清單可能無法顯示清單中所有項目的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-526">Fixed an issue when the Office language was set to Spanish, in which data validation lists may not show all the items in the list.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-527">修正可能會導致「嘗試計算一個或多個公式時，Excel 資源不足」的錯誤問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-527">Fixed an issue which could cause an error that "Excel ran out of resources while attempting to calculate one or more formulas".</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-528">修正在使用資料編輯列輸入公式時，在某些情況下 ChartSheet 出現當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-528">Fixed an issue where ChartSheet crashed in some cases when a formula is entered through formula bar.</span></span>


### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-529">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-529">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-530">當使用者將電子郵件地址複製貼上到顯示名稱的 [收件者] 欄位時，電子郵件地址不一定可被正確分析，並導致出現了一個顯示電子郵件地址無效的警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-530">When a user copy-and-pastes an email address into the recipient field with the display name, the email address wasn't always parsed correctly and caused a warning about an invalid email address to appear.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-531">已修正此問題，可正確分析名稱和電子郵件地址，因此不會再顯示警告。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-531">It's been fixed so the name and email address are parsed correctly so the warning is no longer shown.</span></span>


### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-532">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-532">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-533">修正當使用者在點擊追蹤的變更（插入/刪除）時，會彈出註解的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-533">Fixed an issue where a user tapping on a tracked change (insertion/deletion) would bring up a comment pop-out.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-534">我們已修正 Word 中刪除註解圖說文字的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-534">We fixed an issue with deleting comment callouts in Word.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-535">我們已修正 Outlook 有關將郵件設定為 [不要轉寄] 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-535">We fixed an issue with Outlook with message set to Do not forward.</span></span>


- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-536">我們已修正有關儲存含有引文和方程式的 Word 文件問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-536">We fixed an issue with saving Word document that contains citation and equation.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-571">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-571">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-572">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-572">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-573">修正在啟用「分頁預覽」時，在含有大量資料的工作表之間切換時，可能會發生明顯延遲的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-573">Fixed an issue where there could be a noticeable delay when switching between worksheets with large amounts of data when 'Page Break Preview' was enabled.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-574">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-574">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-575">我們已修正關閉 [焦點收件匣] 並執行排序之後，電子郵件遭隱藏的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-575">We fixed an issue with emails being hidden after turning Focused Inbox off and doing a sort.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-594">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-594">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-596">我們已修正一個問題, 即如果您開啟包含LET 函數的檔案，它會顯示警示：”我們在您的檔案.xlsx 中發現內容有問題”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-596">We fixed an issue where if you opened a file containing the LET function, it would display the alert:  "We found a problem with content in "your file.xlsx".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-597">您想要我們儘量嘗試復原嗎？</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-597">Do you want us to try to recover as much as we can?</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-598">如果您信任這個活頁簿的來源，請按一下 [是]。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-598">If you trust the source of this workbook, click Yes".</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-599">我們已修正與 XLAM 增益集參照和命名範圍相關的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-599">We fixed a crash related to XLAM add-in references and named ranges.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-600">我們修正了使用者無法修改樞紐分析表篩選的問題，因為它已設定為Analysis Services數據庫中不再存在的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-600">We fixed an issue where users could not modify a PivotTable filter because it was set to a value that was no longer present in an Analysis Services database.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-601">我們已修正一個問題: 如果使用者將自訂樣式套用至動態陣列, 他們則會收到錯誤提示：「您無法變更陣列的一部分」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-601">We fixed an issue where if a user applied a custom style to a dynamic array, they would get the error: "You can't change part of an array".</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-602">這是舊版限制，已移除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-602">This was a legacy restriction that has been removed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-603">我們已修正 Excel 公式列與設備失去連線後無法完全呈現的問題，例如遠端會話的連線/斷線或監視器變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-603">We fixed an issue where the Excel formula bar would not render completely after connection to a device was lost, such as a remote session connect/disconnect or a monitor change.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-604">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-604">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-605">我們已修正一個問題, 讓您可透過群組政策來啟用/停用預設的登入選項。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-605">We fixed an issue which provides more flexibility in enabling / disabling the default logging options via Group Policy.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-606">我們已修正電子郵件草稿在助理和經理權限移動時, 寄件者的舊網域名稱仍被保留和顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-606">We fixed an issue where the Legacy Domain Name for an email sender was preserved and displayed after a draft of the email was moved between mailboxes with assistant permissions and manager permissions.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-607">我們已修正一個問題，其導致某些使用者看到 Outlook 在離線狀態下啟動，直到他們手動選擇線上工作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-607">We fixed an issue that caused some users to see Outlook to start in an Offline state until they manually chose to work online.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-608">我們已修正在啟用單行功能區（SLR）後，執行 VBA 程式碼 ActiveInspector （"ShowSchedulingPage"）會導致執行階段錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-608">We fixed an issue where running the VBA code ActiveInspector.CommandBars.ExecuteMso("ShowSchedulingPage") after enabling the Single Line Ribbon (SLR) would result in a runtime error.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-609">我們已修正一個問題, 即Automatic Replies自動回復對話方塊上的確定和取消按鈕以高解析度（例如 1750 x 1920）及較大文字（例如175%）顯示的系統上的錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-609">We fixed an issue where the 'OK' and 'Cancel' buttons on the Automatic Replies dialog would not be visible on a system with a high resolution (such as 1750 x 1920) combined with a large text size (such as 175%).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-610">我們修正一個情況, 即將會議請求從空的聯繫人群組發送到另一個聯繫人組會導致當機。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-610">We fixed a condition where sending a meeting request from an empty contact group to another contact group would result in a crash.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-611">我們解決了導致使用者在打開某些很大的電子郵件時發生當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-611">We fixed an issue that caused users to experience a crash when opening certain very large emails.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-612">我們已修正一個問題, 它使的群組政策要求始終啟用增益集, 則 監視增益集的功能則無法使用，以防止使用者禁用增益集,。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-612">We fixed an issue where if Group Policy requires an Add-in to be always enabled, then monitoring add-in's becomes unavailable in order to prevent users from disabling the Add-in.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-653">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-653">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-654">存取</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-654">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-655">我們已修正 ODBC 資料庫的連線對協力廠商應用程式沒有作用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-655">We fixed an issue where connections to an ODBC database were not working with third party applications.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-656">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-656">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-657">我們已修正使用巨集來設定某個範圍的 FormulaR1C1 屬性時，如果圖表工作表為作用中工作表，則儲存格參考會不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-657">We fixed an issue where using a macro to set the FormulaR1C1 property for a range, the cell references would be incorrect if a chart sheet was the active sheet.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-658">我們已修正筆跡會導致 Excel 無法回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-658">We fixed an issue where inking could cause Excel to become unresponsive.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-659">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-659">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-660">我們已修正一個問題，使用者現在可以停用 Outlook 的 IRM (資訊版權管理)，而不需要為其餘 Office 應用程式停用它。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-660">We fixed an issue where users can now disable IRM (Information Rights Management) for Outlook without having to disable it for the rest of the Office applications.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-754">解決會導致在 S/MIME 加密郵件的頁首中無法顯示鎖定圖示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-754">Addresses an issue that caused the lock icon to fail to display in the header of S/MIME encrypted messages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-755">解決當傳送未加密郵件時，會導致附件從 S/MIME 郵件中剝離出來的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-755">Addresses an issue that caused attachments to get stripped from S/MIME messages when sent unencrypted.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-756">解決當純文字 S/MIME 郵件在傳送時發生亂碼的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-756">Addresses an issue that caused plain text S/MIME messages to become garbled when sending.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-757">解決當傳送未加密的 S/MIME 電子郵件時，會導致附件損毀的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-757">Addresses an issue that caused attachments to become corrupted when sending an S/MIME email unencrypted.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-758">解決選取安全性對話方塊上的 [儲存] 選項時，會導致使用者無法將來自其租用戶外部的 OneDrive 附件儲存至其本機電腦的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-758">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to save OneDrive attachments from outside their tenant to their local computer when selecting the 'Save' option on the security dialog.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-759">解決當寄件者授與 [另存為] 許可權時，會導致收件者無法儲存許可權保護郵件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-759">Addresses an issue that caused recipients to be unable to save rights protected messages even when the save as permission was granted by the sender.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-760">解決某些 [進階搜尋] 選項標籤在某些語言中會被截斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-760">Addresses an issue that caused the labels for some Advanced Search options to be truncated in some languages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-832">我們已修正將插入可縮放向量圖形 (SVG) 中的文字插入到 Word、Excel 或 PowerPoint 檔案、儲存並關閉檔案，然後重新開啟檔案後，難以辨識的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-832">We fixed an issue where text inserted in a Scalable Vector Graphic (SVG) was illegible after inserting it in a Word, Excel, or PowerPoint file, saving and closing the file, and then re-opening the file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-915">我們已修正使用表單型驗證開啟伺服器設定的檔案時發生的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-915">We fixed an issue with opening server-configured files with forms-based authentication.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-916">我們已修正具有內嵌圖表/活頁簿的 PowerPoint 檔案可能會導致儲存檔案失敗的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-916">We fixed an issue where PowerPoint files with embedded charts / workbooks could result in failures when saving the file.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-917">我們已修正使用者關閉的 [註解] 窗格會自動重新開啟的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-917">We fixed an issue where a Comment pane that had been closed by the user would re-open automatically.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-918">我們已修正某張投影片的投影片編輯工具會在下一張投影片上重疊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-918">We fixed an issue where the slide editor from one slide would overlap on to the next slide.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-973">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-973">Resolved issues</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-976">我們已修正管理 Excel 與部分協力廠商輔助技術應用程式之間的字型時發生記憶體損毀的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-976">We fixed an issue where memory was being corrupted when managing fonts between Excel and some third party assistive technology applications.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-977">我們已修正當增益集要求工作表 (包含使用 noSelect 鎖定的圖形) 上的主機項目時，Excel 可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-977">We fixed an issue where Excel would crash when Add-ins ask for Host Items on worksheets that contain shapes with noSelect locks.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1062">修正隱藏和取消隱藏具有系列資料的欄之後，圖表線條樣式可能會遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1062">Fixed an issue where chart line styles could be lost after hiding and unhiding columns with series data.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1065">修正啟用 [負值以補色顯示] 選項後，可能無法儲存樞紐分析表中的自訂格式設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1065">Fixed the issue where custom formatting in Pivot charts may not be saved when the "Invert if negative" option was enabled.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1066">修正如果選取 [負值以補色顯示] 選項，可能無法儲存樞紐分析表中單一資料點的自訂格式設定的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1066">Fixed an issue where custom formatting for a single data point in a Pivot chart was not saved if the "Invert if negative" option was selected.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1067">這項變更修正在 CSV 檔案中上傳 '@' 字元時，會導致將 '@' 字元之後的字串轉換成公式的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1067">This change fixes an issue where the '@' character uploaded in a CSV file, would result in the string after the '@' character to be converted to a formula.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1068">修正無法正確捨入 SEQUENCE 函數中十進位值的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1068">Fixed an issue where decimal values in the SEQUENCE function were not rounded correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1069">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1069">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1070">解決導致使用者在 Outlook 桌面用戶端中按一下非常長的安全連結時，由於截斷而無法載入的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1070">Addresses an issue that caused very long safelinks that users clicked on in the Outlook Desktop client to fail to load due to truncation.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1071">修正當與伺服器同步處理時，名稱中包含 DBCS (雙位元組字元集) 字元的 Outlook 資料夾會間斷消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1071">Fixed an issue where Outlook folders with names containing DBCS (Double Byte Character Set) characters would intermittently disappear when synchronizing with the server.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1072">為此，必須為 Outlook 設定 IMAP 帳戶，並在地區設定設定為日文的系統上執行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1072">For this to happen, Outlook had to be configured with an IMAP account and running on a system with the locale set to Japanese.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1073">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1073">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1074">已修正問題：如果使用者建立了註解，但未張貼就關閉 [註解] 窗格，然後開啟新視窗、瀏覽多張投影片並關閉視窗，最後再開啟原始簡報中的 [註解] 窗格，將導致無法使用草稿註解。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1074">Fixed an issue where if a user created a comment without posting it and closed the Comments pane, then opened a new window, navigated through multiple slides and, closed the window, and finally re-opened the Comments pane in the original presentation, the draft comments would not be available.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1077">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1077">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1080">修正問題：關閉具有草稿註解的文件時，會在不儲存草稿註解的情況下，提示使用者是否要關閉文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1080">Fixed the issue where closing a document with draft comments would prompt the user if they wanted to close the document without saving the draft comments.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1081">取消提示會關閉文件，而不是保持文件開啟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1081">Cancelling the prompt would close the document rather than leaving it open.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1082">修正翻譯已張貼註解將導致「插入已翻譯的文字失敗」錯誤的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1082">Fixed an issue where translating a posted comment would result in the error "Inserting translated text failed".</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1083">在 Web 檢視/沉浸式閱讀器中，如果已在檢視中，按一下提示會捲動到最上方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1083">In Web View/Immersive reader, clicking on a hint would scroll to the top even though it was already in view.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1084">已修正這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1084">This has been fixed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1085">我們已修正一個問題，當嘗試使用新名稱儲存包含巨集的檔案時，無論使用者輸入什麼名稱，都會導致該檔案以.docx 副檔名和檔案名稱 WRO0004.docx 儲存，進而導致文件無法使用。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1085">We fixed an issue that, when attempting to save a file containing a macro under a new name, would cause it to be saved with .docx extension and the filename WRO0004.docx, regardless of what the user entered, rendering the document unusable.</span></span>

## <a name="version-2005-april-24"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1087">版本 2005：4 月 24 日</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1087">Version 2005: April 24</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1088">版本 2005 (組建 12816.20006)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1088">*Version 2005 (Build 12816.20006)*</span></span>

[//]: # (DO NOT REMOVE BUGDETAILS CONTENT START)

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1090">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1090">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1091">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1091">Excel</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1092">這項變更修正了即使 LINEST 函式傳回正確的值，圖表趨勢線的 R 平方值 (在強制 y 截距的情況下) 仍然不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1092">This change fixes an issue where the chart trendline R-Squared value (in the forced y-intercept case) was incorrect even though the LINEST function returns the correct value.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1093">此變更修正了自訂圖表趨勢線格式不一定會儲存的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1093">This change fixes an issue where customized chart trendline formatting was not always being saved.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1094">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1094">Outlook</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1095">修正了 Office 功能區中群組行事曆分類按鈕已停用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1095">Fixed an issue where the Categorize button for group calendars in the Office Ribbon was disabled.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1096">修正了企業客戶沒有執行或無法使用群組資料夾的問題，該問題會導致 Outlook 顯示「沒有回應」的訊息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1096">Fixed an issue where enterprise customers with group folders not implemented or not working, would result in Outlook displaying a "not responding" message.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1097">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1097">PowerPoint</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1098">修正了將滑鼠游標移到星號 (\*) 符號，但不會顯示上一次更新文件的日期和使用者姓名。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1098">Fixed an issue where hovering over the asterisk (\*) symbol did not display the user name and date of the last person to update the document.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1099">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1099">Word</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1100">啟用「顯示書簽」選項卻不會顯示書簽。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1100">Enabling the option "Show bookmarks" would not display bookmarks.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1101">已修正這個問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1101">This has been fixed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1102">此變更修正了下列問題：如果已啟用 [顯示功能變數代碼，而非其值] 選項，則含有超連結的文字可能不會顯示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1102">This change fixes an issue where text with hyperlinks may not display if the option "Show field codes instead of their values" was enabled.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1107">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1107">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1108">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1108">Excel</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1109">已增加搭配圖表使用的 [自訂誤差線] 對話方塊上儲存格參照 [編輯] 控制項的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1109">Increased the size of the cell reference edit controls on the Custom Error Bars dialog used with charts.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1110">在 Excel 2016 中使用數位簽章所儲存的活頁簿，會在於目前版本的 Excel 中開啟時導致簽章失效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1110">Workbooks saved with a digital signature in Excel 2016 could have the signature invalidated upon opening in the current version of Excel.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1111">修正列印時表單控制項的核取方塊縮放問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1111">Fixed a problem with the scaling of checkboxes in form controls when printed.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1112">在某些情況下，Application.Evaluate (VBA) 無法在使用者定義的函數中運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1112">Application.Evaluate (VBA) was not working for User-defined functions in some cases.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1113">此變更會修正設定格式化的條件 (CF) 資訊無法正確儲存到 XLSB 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1113">This change fixes an issue where conditional formatting (CF) information was not being saved to XLSB files correctly.</span></span>

### <a name="onenote"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1114">OneNote</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1114">OneNote</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1115">修正將分行符號儲存為垂直 Tab 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1115">Fixed an issue where line breaks were being stored as vertical tabs.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1116">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1116">Outlook</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1117">解決會導致使用者無法將個人連絡人群組新增為會議出席者的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1117">Addresses an issue that caused users to be unable to add a Personal Contact Group as a Meeting attendee.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1118">解決會導致還有 2 個月時間的會議，無法在排程小幫手中顯示會議主題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1118">Addresses an issue that caused meetings that are more than 2 months away to fail to display a meeting subject in the Scheduling Assistant.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1119">解決會導致使用者在轉寄大型 HTML 郵件時看到郵件內文截斷的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1119">Addresses an issue that caused users to see message body truncation when forwarding large HTML messages.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1120">新增透過群組原則強制執行 S/MIME 預設登入設定的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1120">Added the ability to enforce S/MIME default signing configuration via group policy.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1121">解決會導致為使用者主要信箱以外的信箱所建立的刪除規則變得無效的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1121">Addresses an issue that caused delete rules created for mailboxes other than the user's primary mailbox to become invalid.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1122">解決在轉寄加密郵件時導致捨棄附件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1122">Addresses an issue that caused attachments to get dropped when forwarding an encrypted message.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1123">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1123">Project</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1124">在表單檢視中編輯前置/後續任務資料時，會觸發額外的 ProjectBeforeTaskChange 事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1124">When Predecessor/Successor data is edited within a Form view, an extra ProjectBeforeTaskChange event is fired.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1125">修正變更連結至 SharePoint 工作清單之專案的面板狀態欄位時，Project 可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1125">Fixed an issue where Project may crash when changing the board status field on a project that is connected to a SharePoint task list.</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1126">修正儲存使用舊版 Project 建立的專案時，Project 可能當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1126">Fixed an issue where Project may crash when saving projects created with older versions of Project.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1152">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1152">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1153">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1153">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1154">修正工作窗格中表格的重新調整及重新整理問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1154">Fixed issues with resizing and refreshing tables in the task pane.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1155">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1155">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1156">修正在工作表上選取儲存格範圍會導致只選取單一儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1156">Fixed an issue where selecting a range of cells on a sheet would result in the selection of a single cell.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1157">修正在為含有 X 軸範圍的圖表縮減大小時，可能會導致 Excel 停止回應的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1157">Fixed an issue which could cause Excel to stop responding when reducing the size of a chart with some x-axis ranges.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1158">修正插入使用者定義的圖表範本來作為預設值會導致其儲存為直條圖的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1158">Fixed an issue where inserting a user defined chart template as default would result in saving it as a column chart.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1159">修正當基礎資料儲存格沒有標題時，圖表上的資料標籤會以空白顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1159">Fixed an issue where Data labels on charts would display as blank when the underlying data cells did not have a caption.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1160">修正已啟用 R1C1 儲存格參照且正在共同撰寫/共用的 Excel 工作表，在將游標移到 [使用者目前狀態] 圖示上方時不會以 R1C1 模式顯示作用中儲存格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1160">Fixed an issue where an Excel sheet with R1C1 cell referencing enabled and is being co-authored / shared, hovering over the user presence icon does not display the active cell reference in R1C1 mode.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1161">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1161">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1162">解決會導致類別有時候會從電子郵件訊息中消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1162">Addresses an issue that caused categories to occasionally disappear from email messages.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1163">解決會導致代理人在不同機器上所看到的共用信箱有不同資料夾階層的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1163">Addresses an issue that caused delegates to see different folder hierarchies on different machines for shared mailboxes.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1164">解決在嘗試檢視組織表單的屬性時，會導致使用者遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1164">Addresses an issue that caused users to experience a crash when attempting to view the properties of an Organizational Form.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1165">解決在變更機器上的時區時，會導致某些提醒無法觸發的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1165">Addresses an issue that caused some reminders to fail to fire when changing the timezone on a machine.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1166">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1166">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1167">此變更修正了在 PowerPoint 或 Word 中呈現內嵌為 OLE 物件的舊版 Excel 圖表時可能不會永遠顯示圖表標題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1167">This change fixes an issue where the rendering of a legacy Excel chart embedded as an OLE object in PowerPoint or Word may not always display the chart title.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1168">我們已修正將文字從 Excel 複製到 PowerPoint 時可能會導致其格式設定發生變更的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1168">We have fixed an issue when copying text from Excel to PowerPoint might change its formatting.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1169">此變更修正了使用 [全字拼寫須相符] 來尋找特殊字元時，不一定能正常運作的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1169">This change fixes an issue where finding special characters using 'find whole words only' did not always work as expected.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1170">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1170">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1171">修正了當開啟保護實際工作的設定時，使用者無法輸入分時期基準工時的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1171">Fixed an issue where the user couldn't enter time-phased Baseline Work when the setting to protect actual work is on.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1172">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1172">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1173">此變更修正了將游標暫留在提示上不會醒目提示其卡片的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1173">This change fixes an issue where hovering a cursor over a hint would not highlight its card.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1174">此變更修正了使用套索選取工具時，群組圖形中的文字會暫時消失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1174">This change fixes an issue that would cause the text in grouped shapes to disappear temporarily when using the Lasso selection tool.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1175">此變更修正了在 PowerPoint 或 Word 中呈現內嵌為 OLE 物件的舊版 Excel 圖表時可能不會永遠顯示圖表標題的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1175">This change fixes an issue where the rendering of a legacy Excel chart embedded as an OLE object in PowerPoint or Word may not always display the chart title.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1176">此變更修正了在雙頁檢視中建立註解時，註解錨點不一定會顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1176">This change fixes an issue in two page view, when creating a comment, the comment anchor did not always come into view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1177">修正如果段落的樣式是連結至清單的樣式上階，則該清單的編號可能會遺失的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1177">Fixed an issue where if a paragraph whose style is an ancestor of a style linked to a list, then the numbering of that list could be lost.</span></span>

### <a name="project"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1221">Project</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1221">Project</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1222">已修正當使用者按一下 [排程群組] 內 [工作] 功能區中的 [停用] 按鈕時，不會觸發 'ProjectBeforeTaskChange' Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1222">Fixed an issue where the 'ProjectBeforeTaskChange' Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event did not fire when a user clicked the "Inactivate" button found on the Tasks Ribbon within the Scheduling grouping.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1223">如果您在 [表單類型] 檢視中設定前置任務或後置任務詳細資訊，則 ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) 事件不會一律擷取變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1223">If you set predecessor or successor details from within a Form type view, the ProjectBeforeTaskChange Visual Basic Applications (VBA) event didn't always capture the changes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1224">例如，如果刪除了某個相依性，並在表單上按一下 [確定]，則不會觸發該事件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1224">For example, if you deleted a dependency and clicked OK on the form, the event did not fire.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1225">已修正此問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1225">This behavior has been fixed.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1226">已修正在進行變更 (例如日期變更) 之後，實際工作成本 (ACWP) 的最新值不會顯示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1226">Fixed an issue where the latest values for the Actual Cost of Work Performed (ACWP) would not be displayed after making a change, such as a date change.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1227">已修正使用「最近使用」(MRU) 功能表開啟專案時，會使用 [讀取/寫入] 存取權開啟專案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1227">Fixed an issue where opening a project using the Most Recently Used (MRU) menu opened the project file with Read/Write access.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1228">這項變更修正了如果您建立包含開始日期和時間 (但無工期) 的手動工作，則時間表上的時間顯示不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1228">This change fixes an issue where if you created a manual task with a start date and a time (but no duration), it would be displayed with an incorrect time on the timeline.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1229">已修正使用回曆列印時間表時，會導致列印檢視中略過或重複一個月的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1229">Fixed an issue where printing a timeline using Hijri calendar would result in a month being skipped or duplicated in the print view.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1230">這項變更解決了在團隊規劃中使用 GDI 物件時，可能導致 GDI 物件分配過多並產生記憶體不足的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1230">This change addresses an issue where working in Team Planner with GDI objects, could result in the over allocation of GDI objects and create low memory conditions.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1355">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1355">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1356">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1356">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1357">已解決導致使用者無法存取「空閒/忙碌選項」行事曆權限對話方塊的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1357">Addressed an issue that caused users to lose access to the "Free Busy Options" calendar permissions dialog.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1358">修正了開啟某些從不同時區傳送的週期性會議執行個體時，可能會導致出現警示：「很抱歉，無法開啟這此項目」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1358">Fixed an issue that may result in the alert: "Sorry we're having trouble opening this item" when opening some recurring meeting instances sent from a different time zone.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1359">已解決從該郵件拖放附件後造成使用者無法重新開啟 .msg 檔案的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1359">Addressed an issue that could cause users to be unable to reopen a .msg file after dragging and dropping an attachment from that message.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1360">修正從 Outlook 上傳檔案附件到 OneDrive 後，造成包含括號之附件名稱的檔案名稱被變更。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1360">Fixed an issue where after uploading a file attachment from Outlook to OneDrive could result in the file name being changed if the attachment's name contained parenthesis.</span></span>

### <a name="resolved-issues"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1376">解決的問題</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1376">Resolved issues</span></span>
### <a name="access"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1377">Access</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1377">Access</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1378">此更新會修正使用 ADODB 的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1378">This update fixes an issue where using an ADODB.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1379">VB 程式碼中的記錄器物件可能會不正確地報告錯誤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1379">Recorder object in VB code may incorrectly report an error.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1380">此更新修正可能會導致 Microsoft Access 無法識別連結的 SQL Server 資料表中的識別資料行的問題，這可能會導致不正確地將資料列報告為已刪除。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1380">This update fixes an issue that can cause Microsoft Access to fail to identify an Identity Column in a linked SQL Server table, which can cause rows to be reported as deleted incorrectly.</span></span>

### <a name="excel"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1381">Excel</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1381">Excel</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1382">修正使用「資料剖析」搭配動態陣列時，Excel 會當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1382">Fixed an issue where Excel would crash when using Text To Columns with dynamic arrays.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1383">Outlook</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1383">Outlook</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1384">修正以月檢視在行事曆中捲動時，無法顯示之前的行事曆活動的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1384">Fixed an issue where scrolling in calendar with month view, fails to show previous calendar events.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1385">解決在 Citrix 環境中檢視 30 個以上的行事曆時，導致使用者遇到當機的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1385">Addresses an issue that caused users to experience a crash when viewing more than 30 calendars in a Citrix environment.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1386">PowerPoint</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1386">PowerPoint</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1387">修正關閉檔案之後，如果有任何事件處理常式正在執行，PowerPoint 就不會立即將它從 [簡報] 集合中移除的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1387">Fixed an issue where after closing a file, PowerPoint does not immediately remove it from the Presentations collection if there are any event handlers running.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1388">因此，物件模型報告的開啟中簡報數目會不正確，且會防止關閉 PowerPoint。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1388">Hence the number of open presentations reported by the object model is incorrect, and shutdown of PowerPoint is prevented.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1389">修正具有深色螢光筆色彩的白色文字，在灰階中會以黑色列印的螢光筆問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1389">Fixed an issue with highlighter : White texts with dark highlighter colors are printed as black in Grayscale.</span></span>

### <a name="word"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1390">Word</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1390">Word</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1391">更新和瀏覽目錄時，有時可能會在文件上顯示灰色區域的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1391">Updating and scrolling through a table of contents may sometimes display a gray area over the document.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1392">修正共同撰寫文件時，可能不會保留根註解的草稿版本的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1392">Fixed an issue where if a document is being coauthored, the draft version of a root comment may not be preserved.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1393">已修正在註解卡片之間來回切換時，有時會顯示一開始選取的註解，並將某選取範圍醒目提示的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1393">Fixed an issue where going back and forth between comment cards would sometimes display the initially selected comment with a selection highlight.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1394">修正在已撰寫註解但未張貼，且使用者嘗試儲存檔案的情況下，使用 [瀏覽] 來儲存檔案沒有作用的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1394">Fixed an issue where using 'Browse' to save a file did not work if a comment was written but not posted and the user tried to save the file.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1395">將 SlideTrack 啟用且 [註解] 窗格關閉時，Ctrl+Alt+M 可能無法開啟 [註解] 窗格的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1395">With SlideTrack enabled and the comments pane closed, Ctrl+Alt+M may not open the comments pane.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1396">修正在表格中新增 @提及時可能發生錯誤訊息：「文件中的表格已經毀損」的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1396">Fixed an issue when adding @mention in a table could generate the error message: 'A table in this document has become corrupted'.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite"></a><span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1397">Office 套件</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1397">Office Suite</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="c0b70-1398">解決可能導致挪威耐諾斯克 (nn-no) 校訂工具套件安裝不正確的問題。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="c0b70-1398">Resolves an issue that may have caused Norway Nynorsk (nn-no) proofing tools package to be installed incorrectly.</span></span>
